4073 
4074 /* matches(s1, s2) is true if s1 is "approximately" equal to s2.
4075    Any digits after the first required_precision digits do not have to match.
4076  */
4077 
4078 int required_precision = 13;
4079 
4080 static int
4081 matches (char *result, const char *desired)
4082 {
4083     int digits_seen = 0;
4084     for (;; result++, desired++) {
4085     if (*result == *desired) {
4086         if (*result == 0)
4087         return 1;
4088         else if (*result >= '0' && *result <= '9')
4089         digits_seen++;
4090     }
4091     else if (digits_seen >= required_precision
4092          && *result >= '0' && *result <= '9'
4093          && *desired >= '0' && *desired <= '9')
4094         continue;
4095     else
4096         return 0;
4097     }
4098 }
4099 
4100 int main(int argc, char *argv[])
4101 {
4102   int errcount = 0;
4103   int testcount = 0;
4104   double d;
4105 #define BSIZE 1024
4106   char buffer[BSIZE];
4107   sprint_double_type *dptr;
4108   for (dptr = sprint_doubles; dptr->line; dptr++)
4109     {
4110       sprintf (buffer, dptr->format_string, dptr->value);
4111       if (!matches(buffer, dptr->result))
4112     {
4113       errcount++;
4114       printf(
4115    "Error in line %d using \"%s\".  Result is \"%s\"; should be: \"%s\".\n",
4116           dptr->line, dptr->format_string, buffer, dptr->result);
4117     }
4118 
4119       sprintf (buffer, "%.999g", dptr->value);
4120       sscanf (buffer, "%lg", &d);
4121       if (dptr->value != d && !isnan(d))
4122     {
4123       errcount++;
4124       printf ("Error in line %d.  String is \"%s\", value is %g.\n",
4125           dptr->line, buffer, d);
4126     }
4127       testcount++;
4128     }
4129 
4130   /* And one special test.  */
4131   {
4132     static const char ref[] = "1.7763568394002504646778106689453125e-15";
4133     int i;
4134     d = 1.0;
4135     for (i = 1; i < 50; ++i)
4136       d /= 2;
4137     sprintf (buffer, "%.100g", d);
4138     if (!matches (buffer, ref))
4139       {
4140     ++errcount;
4141     printf (
4142     "Error in line %d using \"%s\".  Result is \"%s\"; should be: \"%s\".\n",
4143         __LINE__, "%.100g", buffer, ref);
4144       }
4145   }
4146 
4147   if (errcount == 0)
4148     {
4149       printf("Encountered no errors in %d tests.\n", testcount);
4150       return 0;
4151     }
4152   else
4153     {
4154       printf("Encountered %d errors in %d tests.\n",
4155           errcount, testcount);
4156       return 1;
4157     }
4158 }
